<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:tanger.html>Tanger</a></i>  + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ine</i>, after <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tangier" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Tangier">Tangier</a>, Morocco.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tangerine.html>tangerine</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tangerines</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of several varieties of mandarin <a href = vnd.unilang:oranges.html>oranges</a>.</li>
<li>A deep yellowish-orange colour, like that of a <a href = vnd.unilang:tangerine.html>tangerine</a> fruit.
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel"><a href = vnd.unilang:tangerine.html>tangerine</a> colour: <span style="background-color:F28500; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A tree that produces tangerines.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Citrus_tangerinaEnglish" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Citrus tangerina"><i>Citrus tangerina</i></a></span></span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms hypernym"><span class="defdate">Hypernym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">mandarin orange</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tangerine.html>tangerine</a></strong>
</p>

***tapas.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tapas.html>tapas</a> (59033)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:tapas.html>tapas</a></i>, plural of <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">tapa</i>, with original sense of “top”.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tapas.html>tapas</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>A variety of Spanish small food <a href = vnd.unilang:items.html>items</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:snacks.html>snacks</a>, originally served with <a href = vnd.unilang:sherry.html>sherry</a>.
<ul><li><b>1986</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jeff_Smith_(TV_personality)" class="extiw" title="w:Jeff Smith (TV personality)"><a href = vnd.unilang:jeff.html>Jeff</a> Smith</a>, <i>The Frugal Gourmet Cooks with Wine</i>
<dl><dd>The <a href = vnd.unilang:snacks.html>snacks</a> are called <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tapas.html>tapas</a></b> because in the old days a piece of <a href = vnd.unilang:toast.html>toast</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> served, too, so that you might have a "top" on your glass of <a href = vnd.unilang:sherry.html>sherry</a>, a <a href = vnd.unilang:lid.html>lid</a> that would prevent the flies from getting into the glass.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Small food <a href = vnd.unilang:items.html>items</a> generally.
<dl><dd><i>Izakaya food <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> basically Japanese <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tapas.html>tapas</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">small plate</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">small plates</span> (see <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/small_plates" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:small plates">small plates</a>)</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tapas.html>tapas</a></b>  <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">mv</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:meervoud.html>meervoud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a> tapa</li></ol>
<hr><h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synoniemen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:synoniemen.html>Synoniemen</a></i></span></h5>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tappen.html>tappen</a></i>. <ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:techniek.html>techniek</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:vloeistof.html>vloeistof</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vat.html>vat</a> of leidingbuis, in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:glas.html>glas</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:emmer.html>emmer</a> etc.  <a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stromen.html>stromen</a>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">tap</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(<a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a>) tap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">closed, shut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***tarmac.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tarmac.html>tarmac</a> (72551)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Clipping of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tarmacadam</i></span></span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tar</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">macadam</i> (crushed stones). Originally a trademark owned by its inventor <a href = vnd.unilang:edgar.html>Edgar</a> Hooley.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tarmac.html>tarmac</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tarmacs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Tarmacadam.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">loosely<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canada" class="extiw" title="w:Canada">Canada</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any bituminous road surfacing material.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1922</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michael_Arlen" class="extiw" title="w:Michael Arlen">Michael Arlen</a>,  “3/1/1”, in  <cite>“Piracy”: A Romantic Chronicle of These Days</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL1519647W">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">How meek and shrunken <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> that haughty <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tarmac.html>Tarmac</a></b> become as it slunk by the wide circle of asphalt of the yellow sort, that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> loosely strewn before the great iron gates of Lady Hall as a forerunner of the consideration that awaited the guests of Rupert, <a href = vnd.unilang:earl.html>Earl</a> of Kare, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">asphalt</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canada" class="extiw" title="w:Canada">Canada</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The driveable surface of a road.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The area of an airport, other than the runway, where <a href = vnd.unilang:planes.html>planes</a> park or maneuver.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tarmac.html>tarmac</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">tarmacs</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tarmacking</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tarmacing</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tarmaccing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tarmacked</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tarmaced</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tarmacced</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canada" class="extiw" title="w:Canada">Canada</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To pave with tarmacadam or a similar material.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2008</b>,  Valerie Belsey,  <cite>Exploring Green <a href = vnd.unilang:lanes.html>Lanes</a> in North and North-West <a href = vnd.unilang:devon.html>Devon</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=HOfx3m2wT2kC">[2]</a></sup>, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 108:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">To your left <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a green lane, partly <b>tarmacked</b> with chippings, which leads up to a little car-parking area.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>2014</b>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.itv.com/news/granada/update/2014-05-29/taking-the-rough-with-the-smooth-bolton-residents-anger-over-half-tarmaced-road/">Taking the rough with the smooth: Bolton residents anger <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> half-tarmaced road</a>, ITV Granada:
<dl><dd>Residents in Bolton are angry after workmen <b>tarmaced</b> only one <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> of their road leaving the other <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> strewn with potholes.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To spend time idling on a runway, usually waiting for takeoff clearance.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1989</b>,  Donald F. Wood amp; James C. Johnson,  <cite>Contemporary Transportation</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=nS1PAAAAMAAJ">[3]</a></sup>, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 213:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not unusual these days for the time spent <b>tarmacking</b> to exceed the time spent in the air, " <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:senator.html>Senator</a> John Danforth, R-Mo.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tarpon.html>tarpon</a> (72550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">tarpoen</i>. Suggestions that the term derives from a Native American term<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> are unlikely.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tarpon.html>tarpon</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tarpons</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:tarpon.html>tarpon</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of several <a href = vnd.unilang:fishes.html>fishes</a> of the family <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Elopidae" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Elopidae">Elopidae</a></span> or Megalopidae, especially a large silvery game fish.</li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tas.html>tas</a> (1201)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tassche</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tasche</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*taskǭ</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">tasca</i> (modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Tasche</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">taske</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tasse</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li>bag

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">tasse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">طَاس</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ṭās</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (a shortening of <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">طَسْت</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ṭast</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Persian" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Persian">Middle Persian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pal">tšt'</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="pal-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tašt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tas.html>tas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tassen.html>tassen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tasje.html>tasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cup (like a cup of coffee or tea)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">cup</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kopje.html>kopje</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mok.html>mok</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jat.html>jat</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tas.html>tas</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tasse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:tas.html>tas</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tasso</i>, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:tas.html>tas</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tass.html>tass</a></i> (from Frankish), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tassaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pile, heap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dāy-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to divide, split, section, part, separate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***tass.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tass.html>tass</a> (87535)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Partly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:tas.html>tas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">heap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:tas.html>tas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">heap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:tas.html>tas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mass, pile</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; and partly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">taas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">heap, mow of corn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:tas.html>tas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">heap, mow of grain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; both from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tasaz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tassaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">heap, mow, stack</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*deh₂y-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to divide, split, section, part, separate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tas.html>tas</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tasse</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">heap, pile</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, <span class="ann-pos"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tas.html>tas</a></i></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:tas.html>tas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mow of hay or wheat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌿𐌽𐌲𐌰𐍄𐌰𐍃𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ungatass</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">disorganised, irregular</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; and possibly also to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:zetten.html>zetten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to straw, fertilise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">tað</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spread dung</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See <span class="Latn" lang="en">tath</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tass.html>tass</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tasses</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> or obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A heap, pile.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*tasse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">tasse</i> (Modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">tasse</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cup, cupful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tas.html>tas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cup</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Tasse</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mug</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tazza</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tass.html>tass</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tasses</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_England" class="extiw" title="w:Northern England">Northern England</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cup or cupful.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1824</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:walter.html>Walter</a> Scott,  <cite>Redgauntlet</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"Here, Dougal," <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> the <a href = vnd.unilang:laird.html>Laird</a>, "gie Steenie a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tass.html>tass</a></b> of <a href = vnd.unilang:brandy.html>brandy</a> down stairs, till I count the siller and write the receipt."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">tasse</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">tache</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">tasse</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">tasche</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">purse; pouch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*taska</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pouch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*taskǭ</i>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">tasca</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pouch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Tasche</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pocket; pouch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tass.html>tass</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tasses</b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tastbaar.html>tastbaar</a> (27928)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tast.html>tast</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tasten.html>tasten</a></i></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-baar</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:taw.html>taw</a> (44542)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">tawen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">tawian</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to do, make</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tawjaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to make, prepare</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dewh₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to tie to, secure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:touwen.html>touwen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rope, tether, curry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">tuien</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fasten with ropes</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:tau.html>Tau</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rope, hawser, cable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐍄𐌰𐌿𐌾𐌰𐌽</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taujan</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to make, prepare</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tool</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tether</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:taw.html>taw</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">taws</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tawing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tawed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To prepare or dress, as hemp, by beating; to tew.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To beat; to scourge.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To dress and prepare, as the <a href = vnd.unilang:skins.html>skins</a> of sheep, <a href = vnd.unilang:lambs.html>lambs</a>, goats, and kids, for gloves, etc., by imbuing them with alum, salt, and other agents, for softening and bleaching them.
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To turn (animals' hide) into leather, usually by soaking it in a certain solution.</li></ol></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">tool</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:taw.html>taw</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Tawed leather.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:taw.html>taw</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">taws</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A favorite marble in the game of <a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a>.
<ul><li><b>1922</b> , <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Joyce" class="extiw" title="w:James Joyce">James Joyce</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ulysses" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ulysses">Ulysses</a></i>, chapter V:<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/ebooks/4300">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd><i>Near the timberyard a squatted child at <a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a>, alone, shooting the <a href = vnd.unilang:taw.html>taw</a> with a cunnythumb.</i></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A line or mark from which the players begin a game of <a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">square dancing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A dance partner.
<dl><dd><i>Walk around your corner; see-saw around your <b><a href = vnd.unilang:taw.html>taw</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>A favorite person; beloved, partner, spouse.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:taw.html>taw</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">taws</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tawing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tawed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To shoot a marble.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:taw.html>taw</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">taws</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The 22nd and last letter of many Semitic alphabets/abjads, including Phoenician, Aramaic, Hebrew, Syriac<span class="serial-comma">,</span> and Arabic.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tew</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to tow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tow</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:taw.html>taw</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">taws</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tawing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tawed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To push; to tug; to tow.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Drayton to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Initialism of its component <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschikking.html>beschikking</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stelling.html>stelling</a></i>. Because the initialism <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> more common than the full form, it can be considered to be an anacronym.

***td.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> td (11072)</h1><br></body> 
***te.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> (21)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_8">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ta</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>too <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">indicating excess</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>Te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nooit.html>nooit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">too much <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> never good</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gek.html>gek</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">far out!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_3">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">modifying an infinitive verb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>eten</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> something to eat</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>located at, in, on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>Te</a></b> Amsterdam</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">in Amsterdam.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rijden.html>rijden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:paard.html>paard</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">and so <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> ride on horseback.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Article">Article</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> in idiom; a form of the definite article <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>Te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drommel.html>drommel</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">by <a href = vnd.unilang:jove.html>Jove</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This preposition used to govern the dative case. It also fused with the dative forms of the definite article:
</p>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at, in</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a></span> = <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> + <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a></span> for feminine singular.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at, in</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">ten</span> = <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> + <span class="Latn" lang="nl">den</span> in all other <a href = vnd.unilang:cases.html>cases</a>.</li></ul>
<p>Combinations with the nominative form of the article, like *<i><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i> or *<i><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i> have never become part of the language. The collapse of the inflection system and the related demise of the distinction between masculine and feminine gender (for most <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pushed.html>pushed</a> this preposition into partial disuse. It does however occur in a fair number of idiomatic expressions, often with fossilized case <a href = vnd.unilang:endings.html>endings</a>, e.g.:
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> elfder <a href = vnd.unilang:ure.html>ure</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">at the eleventh hour</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:eigen.html>eigen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bate.html>bate</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">for one's own profit</span></div></dd></dl>
<p>(<i>Elfder</i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ure.html>ure</a></i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bate.html>bate</a></i> are dative forms of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elfde.html>elfde</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>uur</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baat.html>baat</a></i> respectively.)
</p>
<hr />

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">technique</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τεχνικός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tekhnikós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">of or pertaining to art, artistic, skilful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τέχνη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tékhnē</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">art, handicraft</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τίκτειν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tíktein</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bring forth, produce</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
